## Text Elements
if (mid < mid+1)
    start = mid
else if ( mid < mid - 1)
    end = mid
else 
    return mid ^HRsj0KyQ

if (mid < mid+1)
    start = mid + 1
else 
    end = mid
return mid ^nJEgWAYz
